FILE: README.md
==================================================
# Astro Starter Kit: Minimal

```sh
npm create astro@latest -- --template minimal
```

> 🧑‍🚀 **Seasoned astronaut?** Delete this file. Have fun!

## 🚀 Project Structure

Inside of your Astro project, you'll see the following folders and files:

```text
/
├── public/
├── src/
│   └── pages/
│       └── index.astro
└── package.json
```

Astro looks for `.astro` or `.md` files in the `src/pages/` directory. Each page is exposed as a route based on its file name.

There's nothing special about `src/components/`, but that's where we like to put any Astro/React/Vue/Svelte/Preact components.

Any static assets, like images, can be placed in the `public/` directory.

## 🧞 Commands

All commands are run from the root of the project, from a terminal:

| Command                   | Action                                           |
| :------------------------ | :----------------------------------------------- |
| `npm install`             | Installs dependencies                            |
| `npm run dev`             | Starts local dev server at `localhost:4321`      |
| `npm run build`           | Build your production site to `./dist/`          |
| `npm run preview`         | Preview your build locally, before deploying     |
| `npm run astro ...`       | Run CLI commands like `astro add`, `astro check` |
| `npm run astro -- --help` | Get help using the Astro CLI                     |

## 👀 Want to learn more?

Feel free to check [our documentation](https://docs.astro.build) or jump into our [Discord server](https://astro.build/chat).

        aria-controls="mobile-menu"

      >

<div
  id="mobile-menu"
  class="mobile-menu fixed inset-0 z-40 hidden lg:hidden"
  data-mobile-menu
>
  <button
    type="button"
    class="absolute inset-0 bg-black/45 backdrop-blur-[2px]"
    aria-label="Close menu"
    data-menu-backdrop
  ></button>

  <div class="absolute inset-x-0 top-[76px] border-b border-white/10 bg-neutral-950 px-6 pb-6 pt-4 shadow-2xl">
    <nav class="mx-auto flex max-w-7xl flex-col gap-2" aria-label="Mobile">
      {nav.map((item) => (
        <a
          href={item.href}
          class="rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 text-base text-white/80 transition hover:bg-white/6 hover:text-white"
          data-mobile-link
        >
          {item.label}
        </a>
      ))}
    </nav>
  </div>
</div>

<script is:inline>
  (() => {
    const header = document.querySelector("[data-header]");
    const toggle = document.querySelector("[data-menu-toggle]");
    const menu = document.querySelector("[data-mobile-menu]");
    const links = document.querySelectorAll("[data-mobile-link]");
    const backdrop = document.querySelector("[data-menu-backdrop]");
    const openIcon = toggle?.querySelector("[data-icon-open]");
    const closeIcon = toggle?.querySelector("[data-icon-close]");

    if (!header || !toggle || !menu) return;

    let scrollY = 0;

    const lockScroll = () => {
      scrollY = window.scrollY;
      document.body.style.position = "fixed";
      document.body.style.top = `-${scrollY}px`;
      document.body.style.left = "0";
      document.body.style.right = "0";
      document.body.style.width = "100%";
    };

    const unlockScroll = () => {
      document.body.style.position = "";
      document.body.style.top = "";
      document.body.style.left = "";
      document.body.style.right = "";
      document.body.style.width = "";
      window.scrollTo(0, scrollY);
    };

    const closeMenu = () => {
      header.dataset.menuOpen = "false";
      toggle.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
      menu.classList.add("hidden");
      openIcon?.classList.remove("hidden");
      closeIcon?.classList.add("hidden");
      unlockScroll();
    };

    const openMenu = () => {
      header.dataset.menuOpen = "true";
      toggle.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
      menu.classList.remove("hidden");
      openIcon?.classList.add("hidden");
      closeIcon?.classList.remove("hidden");
      lockScroll();
    };

    const toggleMenu = () => {
      const isOpen = toggle.getAttribute("aria-expanded") === "true";
      isOpen ? closeMenu() : openMenu();
    };

    toggle.addEventListener("click", toggleMenu);
    backdrop?.addEventListener("click", closeMenu);
    links.forEach((link) => link.addEventListener("click", closeMenu));

    window.addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
      if (event.key === "Escape") closeMenu();
    });

    window.addEventListener("resize", () => {
      if (window.innerWidth >= 1024) closeMenu();
    });
  })();
</script>

<script
  is:inline
  define:vars={{
    calOrigin,
  }}
>
  (function () {
    const services = {
      maintenance: {
        label: "Maintenance Detail",
        slug: "factoryresetdetail/maintenance-detail",
        blurb:
          "Best for already well-kept vehicles that need consistent upkeep and preferred recurring pricing.",
      },
      signature: {
        label: "Signature Detail",
        slug: "factoryresetdetail/signature-detail",
        blurb:
          "Best for clients wanting a deeper, more complete detail with stronger interior and wheel attention.",
      },
      reset: {
        label: "Factory Reset Detail",
        slug: "factoryresetdetail/factory-reset-detail",
        blurb:
          "Best for the most comprehensive reset short of correction work, inside and out.",
      },
    };

    const defaultService = "signature";
    const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const serviceParam = params.get("service");
    const activeService = services[serviceParam] ? serviceParam : defaultService;
    const selected = services[activeService];

    const labelEl = document.getElementById("selected-service-label");
    const blurbEl = document.getElementById("selected-service-blurb");

    if (labelEl) labelEl.textContent = selected.label;
    if (blurbEl) blurbEl.textContent = selected.blurb;

    const pillIds = {
      maintenance: "service-pill-maintenance",
      signature: "service-pill-signature",
      reset: "service-pill-reset",
    };

    Object.entries(pillIds).forEach(([key, id]) => {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (!el) return;

      if (key === activeService) {
        el.className =
          "inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white bg-white px-4 py-2 text-sm text-neutral-950 transition";
      } else {
        el.className =
          "inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-4 py-2 text-sm text-white/75 transition hover:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/10";
      }
    });

    function bootCal() {
      if (!window.Cal) return;

      const booker = document.getElementById("cal-booker");
      if (booker) booker.innerHTML = "";

      window.Cal("init", { origin: calOrigin });

      window.Cal("inline", {
        elementOrSelector: "#cal-booker",
        calLink: selected.slug,
        config: {
          layout: "month_view",
          "metadata[selectedService]": selected.label,
        },
      });

      window.Cal("ui", {
  styles: {
    body: {
      background: "#0a0a0a",
    },
  },
});


      window.Cal("on", {
        action: "bookingSuccessfulV2",
        callback: function () {
          const upload = document.getElementById("upload-photos");
          if (upload) {
            upload.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "start" });
          }
        },
      });
    }

    if (window.Cal) {
      bootCal();
      return;
    }

    (function (C, A, L) {
      let p = function (a, ar) { a.q.push(ar); };
      let d = C.document;
      C.Cal =
        C.Cal ||
        function () {
          let cal = C.Cal;
          let ar = arguments;
          if (!cal.loaded) {
            cal.ns = {};
            cal.q = cal.q || [];
            let s = d.createElement("script");
            s.src = A;
            s.async = true;
            d.head.appendChild(s);
            cal.loaded = true;
          }
          if (ar[0] === L) {
            const api = function () { p(api, arguments); };
            const namespace = ar[1];
            api.q = api.q || [];
            if (typeof namespace === "string") {
              cal.ns[namespace] = cal.ns[namespace] || api;
              p(cal.ns[namespace], ar);
            } else {
              p(cal, ar);
            }
            return;
          }
          p(cal, ar);
        };
    })(window, "https://app.cal.com/embed/embed.js", "init");

    bootCal();
  })();
</script>

<script is:inline>
(() => {
  const slideshow = document.querySelector("[data-hero-slideshow]");
  if (!slideshow) return;

  const slides = [...slideshow.querySelectorAll("[data-hero-slide]")];
  const dots = [...slideshow.querySelectorAll("[data-hero-dot]")];

  if (!slides.length || !dots.length) return;

  let current = 0;
  let intervalId;

  const setActive = (index) => {
    current = index;

    slides.forEach((slide, i) => {
      slide.classList.toggle("opacity-100", i === index);
      slide.classList.toggle("opacity-0", i !== index);
    });

    dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
      dot.classList.toggle("w-8", i === index);
      dot.classList.toggle("bg-white", i === index);
      dot.classList.toggle("w-2", i !== index);
      dot.classList.toggle("bg-white/35", i !== index);
      dot.classList.toggle("hover:bg-white/55", i !== index);
    });
  };

  const stop = () => {
    if (intervalId) {
      window.clearInterval(intervalId);
      intervalId = null;
    }
  };

  const start = () => {
    stop();
    intervalId = window.setInterval(() => {
      const next = (current + 1) % slides.length;
      setActive(next);
    }, 5000);
  };

  dots.forEach((dot, index) => {
    dot.addEventListener("click", () => {
      setActive(index);
      start();
    });
  });

  slideshow.addEventListener("mouseenter", stop);
  slideshow.addEventListener("mouseleave", start);

  setActive(0);
  start();
})();
</script>

<style>
.hero-slide {
  transition: opacity 900ms ease;
  will-change: opacity;
}
</style>

<script is:inline>
  (() => {
    const track = document.querySelector("[data-service-track]");
    const slides = [...document.querySelectorAll("[data-service-slide]")];
    const dots = [...document.querySelectorAll("[data-service-dot]")];

    if (!track || !slides.length || !dots.length) return;

    const setActive = (index) => {
      slides.forEach((slide, i) => {
        slide.classList.toggle("border-white/22", i === index);
        slide.classList.toggle("bg-white/[0.06]", i === index);
        slide.classList.toggle("border-white/10", i !== index);
        slide.classList.toggle("bg-white/[0.03]", i !== index);
      });

      dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
        dot.classList.toggle("w-8", i === index);
        dot.classList.toggle("bg-white", i === index);
        dot.classList.toggle("w-2.5", i !== index);
        dot.classList.toggle("bg-white/30", i !== index);
      });
    };

    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
      (entries) => {
        const visible = entries
          .filter((entry) => entry.isIntersecting)
          .sort((a, b) => b.intersectionRatio - a.intersectionRatio)[0];

        if (!visible) return;

        const index = slides.indexOf(visible.target);
        if (index >= 0) setActive(index);
      },
      {
        root: track,
        threshold: 0.65,
      }
    );

    slides.forEach((slide) => observer.observe(slide));

    dots.forEach((dot, index) => {
      dot.addEventListener("click", () => {
        slides[index]?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", inline: "center", block: "nearest" });
      });
    });
  })();
</script>
